 darshakon ke dilon par dashakon se raaj kar raheen 'dream girl' hema malini aaj bhi raajnneeti ke saath-saath abhinay main sakriy hai
 She has left an indelible mark on Hindi cinema with her beauty, acting, romance and bubbly mood
 'haa jab tak he jaan', 'dhire-dhire bol koi sun na le', 'jindagi ek safar he suhana', 'tere chehre main wo jaadu he', 'tuune o rangile' jaise sadabahaar geet sunate hi hema malini kaa cheharaa saamne aa jaataa he
 Hema's film career, coming from South India and soon set foot in Bollywood, has been full of highs
 unka janm 16 oktober, 1948 ko tamilnadu main hua tha
 His mother's name was Jaya Chakraborty and father's name was VSR Chakraborty
 hema ke janm se pehle unki maa itani nishcint thim ki unhone pehle hi apane hone vaali beti kaa naam 'hema malini' soch liya tha
 Mother wanted her daughter to be a good dancer
 hema ne maa kaa yah sapana puraa kar dikhaaya
 She was also very smart in studies
 itihaas unka pasandida vishay rahaa he
 She could not take the 10th grade exams as she was constantly receiving acting offers
 umr maatr chaudaa saal thi, lekin hema ke daravaaje par film nirmaataa tabhi se dastak dene lage the
 In 1981, she tied the knot with actor Dharmendra
 'sholay' film se mashhoor hue dharmendra or hema kii aaysha deol or aahna deol naam kii do betiyaan hai
 Mothers and daughters also offer several charitable programs
 hema se shaadi se pehle dharmendra kii pehali patni prakaash cor se chaar bachche hai
 Dharmendra and Hema Malini have also become maternal grandparents
 unki choti beti ahaana deol ne haal hi main ek bete ko janm diya tha
 Hema Malini's mother Jaya Chakraborty was a Tamil film-maker
 hindi filmon main hema malini ko pehla avasar 'sapanom kaa saudagar' (1968) main mila
 Hema's hero showman was Raj Kapoor, who was much older than Hema in terms of age
 raaj kapur ne us dauraan kaha tha ki hema ek din cinema kii bahut badi star banegi or hema ne unki bhavishyavaanee ko sach kar dikhaaya
 Hema Malini started to be taken seriously with 'johny Mera Naam' released in 1970
 yah film box offis par superhit sabit hui
 Early in his career, Hema did some films with Dharmendra like 'tum Hasin Main Jawaan' (1969), 'sharafat' (1969), 'naya Jamana' (1971)
 ye filmein bhale hi box offis par zyada nahin chali, lekin donon kaa romance parde par or parde ke baahar bakhubi chalaa
 She played two roles in the 1972 film 'sita and Geeta'
 is film kii shandaar kamyaabi ne hema ko badi nayika bana diya
 She came to be known as 'dream Girl'
 isi naam kii ek film hema kii maa ne banaai thi
 The magic of Hema Malini's beauty was also felt on many film actors
 jitendra se lekar sanjeev kumaar jaise abhinayta unase shaadi karnaa chaahate the, lekin baad main unhone dharmendra sang saat phere liye
 In films he was liked alongside Dharmendra, Rajesh Khanna, Jeetendra and Amitabh Bachchan
 ullekhneey he ki varsh 2004 main hema malini bhartiya janata party main shaamil huin or unhone raajnneetik safar shuru kiya
 He has duly trained in Bharatanatyam, Kuchipudi and Odissi and has performed several stage shows in India and abroad
 filmphir awords kii sarvshereshth abhinetri shrenee main hema malini kaa naam 11 baar namankit hua he, lekin unhen keval ek baar sita or gita ke liye hi yah puraskaar mila he
 Hema does yoga and exercises daily to maintain her beauty
 saptaah main do baar upwas unki niyamit jindagi kaa ang he
 One of these days is Friday
 hema ko kanjivaram saadiyaan, chameli ke gajre or dher sari jewelri bhi pasand hai
 Seeing her freshness in the film 'baghban', Amitabh Bachchan said, "even today you look more young than your daughters
 " In the year 1990, Hema Malini also turned to the small screen and also directed the serial Nupur
 iske baad varsh 1992 main film abhinayta shahrukh khan ko lekar unhone film (dil aashna he) kaa nirmaan or nirdesan kiya
 In the year 1995, he produced and directed 'mohini' for small screen
 filmon main kai bhoomikaayen nibhaane ke baad hema malini ne samajaseva ke liye raajnneeti main pravesh kiya or bhartiya janata party ke sahyog se rajyasabha kii sadsy baniin
 Hema Malini was also awarded the Filmfare Lifetime Achishree Award in 1999 for her outstanding contribution to films
 tippaniyan Hema Malini acted in about 150 films in her four-decade cinema career
 unki kuch ullekhneey filmein 'sita or gita', 'prem nagar amir garib', 'sholay','mahabuuba charas', 'dream girl kinaaraa', 'trishul', 'mira', 'kudarat naseeb kranti', 'andhaa kanoon razia sultan', 'rihaai', 'jamaai raja', 'bagban', 'vir jaaraa' jaisi filmon main kaam kiya
 She was also elected as a Rajya Sabha member of the Bharatiya Janata Party
 vartmaan main vah mathura (uttar pradesh) se loksabhaa kii saansad hai
 Happy Birthday to Dream Girl and skilled politician Hema Malini !!! (apart from the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, published directly from Syndicate Feed
 ) He was born on 16 October 1948 in Tamil Nadu
 unki maa kaa naam jaya chakravarti or pita kaa naam viesar chakravarti tha

 maa apni bitiyaa ko acchhee nartki bananaa chaahati thim
 Hema fulfilled this dream of her mother
 vah padhai main bhi kaaphi hoshiyaar thim
 History has been his favorite subject
 vah 10veen kaksha kii pariksha nahin de pain, kyonki unhen lagaataar abhinay ke prastaav mil rahe the

 maa or betiyaan kai cheritable kaarykram bhi prastut karti hai

 'do betiyon kaa pita hone ke naate main ye apni zimmedaari samajhataa hum ki is maamle ko isaki taarkik parinti tak pahunchaaya jaae
 The goons should be punished and the law should do its job
 ye gunde prabhaavshaalee pariwaron se hai
 We all know that in most of such cases the culprits are not punished and in many cases even the reports are not there
 adhiktar log prabhaavshaalee pariwaron ke aise gundon kaa saamana karne se bachate hai
 i think if some privileged people like us do not stand in front of such criminals then no one will be able to stand in India
 isse bhi zyaada agar main is maamle main puri tarah apni beti ke saath khadaa nahin hounga to uskaa pita hone ke apane farz main naakaam rahoonga
 i am sharing this case with you for two reasons
 ek to jo hua uski saafe or sachhee tasviir dene ke liye or doosraa agar zarurat padi to aapke samarthan ke kuch aashwaasan ke liye
 ' iees afasaron kaa ek associesan bhi he
 It has been tweeted by tweeting
 saharanpur main jab esaspi ke ghar raajnneetik bheed ghus ai, or kaaphi der tak esaspi kaa parivaar asurakshit mahasoos karne laga tab ipies association ko pratikriya dene main kai ghante lag gaye
 Perhaps there is a decision that we should show political loyalty or show loyalty to our profession
 unhen bhi pataa he ki ab kuch badalanaa nahin he
 Why react in sentiment, it is better to stick to your political loyalty
 kuch to he ki system na to bheetar waalon ke liye he yaa na baahar waalon ke liye he
 In the system too, all are for those who are with power
 hamaari naukarshahi pichley kai dashakon main sadati rahi he
 Now she is so rotten that moss is falling off the wall
 iees virendra kumaar ne apni beti kaa saath dene kaa faisla kiya he
 The accused son is accompanied by more people than IAS Virender Kumar
 media trial se bachanaa chahie
 But the system must have a media trial
 aap nahin jaanate, ek baar kisi mukademe main ulajhiye, pataa chalegaa ki kis kis mez par aapaki gardan dabochi jaati he
 That is why someone has to declare that he will fight
 jaise hi vah kahata he ki vah ladega, har haal main ladega is matlab yahi he ki wo jaanata he ki yah system use todane kii had tak pahunchaa degaa, phir bhi ladega
 This announcement has its own price
 vakeelon kii fees, tarikhon kaa intazaar
 Relying on justice and justice is not the only thing, it is the cost
 is bharose ko jeetne ke liye paisa lagata he
 Go out of any court and meet the people who have come to win this trust
 aap bhi elaan karne lagenge ki chaahe jo ho jaae, main satya ke liye laduunga
 The comments hamaare sahyogi channel se haryana bijepi ke upaadhyaksh ne baat karte hue jo kaha wo bhi suna janaa chahie
 He said that the government cannot provide security to every citizen
 ham or aap abhi tak isi bharam main the ki sarkaar har naagarik ko suraksha dene kaa vaada karti he lekin yah bhi bharam tut gaya ki sarkaar har naagarik ko suraksha nahin de sakati he
 Now there is no chance to ask the question that when it cannot provide security to every citizen, is it a security system for a select few citizens, is it for the common people, for the political people or for the people of the administration
 duusari baat unhone kahi he ki maa baap apane bacchon kaa khyaal rakhen, unhen raat main ghoomane phirane nahin dena chahie
 Children come home on time, what is the use of walking at night
 is baat par ek faisla ho hi jaae
 The whole of India should be closed at night
 koi shaam ke baad ghar se hi na nikle
 Next, you should listen to his statement
 haryana bijepi ke upaadhyaksh ramvir ji ne kaha he ki chandigarh police dabaav main nahin aegi
 How often the Himachal incident is mentioned in his statement
 thik bhi he lekin yahi raajnneeti he
 Chief Minister Khattar has said that the law will do its job
 putr kii galati kii sazaa pita ko kyon milani chahie
 Those seeking resignation from father also know the state of the system
 unhen pataa he ki is maamle main insaaf milte milte saal guzar jaaenge isliye virdohi kii raajnneeti bhi vahi he jo satta paksh kii raajnneeti he
 That is why the emphasis is on resignation
 taaki raajnneetik dal apana victory cap lekar chalate bane or ladki or uske pita usee chauraahey par khadey rahenge
 If someone says that he has changed this, it is the biggest lie of the last ten thousand years
 varanaa ek senior iees afasar ko yah nahin kahana padataa ki hamaari manshaa he ki aparaadhiyon ko sazaa mili
 We have no desire to harm their families and relatives
 main jaanata hum ki ye ek aasaan sangharsh hone nahin ja rahaa
 There is no denying that we are suspected of harassing, following us, threatening us and causing physical harm
 rasookh vaale parivaar kai baar shikayatakartaaon ko naakaam karne ke liye unhen badnaam karne ke liye kuch bhi kar sakate hai
 May be we are getting very adventurous
 samajhadaar dost hamen aage kii karrwai ke bare main suzav de sakate hai
 Think of an IAS officer who spent many years of his life within this system, which he dreamed of fixing, had to write this
 apni beti ke liye jaise hi ek baap system ke saamne khadaa hota he, wo vaise hi nihattha laachaar ho jaataa he jaise ham or aap
 Thankfully Virendra Kundu wants to stand up for his daughter in every situation
 ham ummid karte hai ki us system main baithe duusare iees afasaraan bhi unka saath denge
 They too will come forward and those officers who have lost their voice for political allegiance will also speak for Virendra's daughter
 aap jaanate hai ki shuukravaar raat jab virendra kundu kii beti chandigarh ke sector saat se apane ghar ke liye nikaleen to safed tata safari peechha karne lagati he
 Varnika has alleged that Tata Safari followed her car for a long time
 ek jagah unki car ke saamne apni car khadi kar di or rasta block kar diya
 After getting out of the car, Vikas Barala's friend Ashish arrives and hits Varnika's car window hard
 daravaaza kholane ke liye kahata he
 Varnika took her car behind and ran through another path
 uske haath paanv thande ho gaye the
 Complaints to the police and the police also come
 police ne khud dekha or ladakon ko pakad kar thane le ai
 Both boys were drunk
 baad main pataa chalaa ki ladki ek iees afasar kii beti he or ladakon main ek haryana bijepi adhyaksh kaa betaa he
 This is where everything changes
 apni beti ke liye ladane aayaa ek pita fasebuk par likhane kaa faisla karata he
 Perhaps he knows that no media should come in this era of dock media
 isliye pita virendra kundu fasebuk par likhte hai
 
 
 'as a father of two daughters, i consider it my responsibility to take the matter to its logical end
 gundon ko har haal main sazaa milani chahie or kaanoon ko apana kaam karnaa chahie
 These goons are from influential families
 ham sab jaanate hai ki aise adhiktar maamalon main doshiyon ko sazaa nahin hoti or kai maamalon main to report tak nahin hoti
 Most people avoid facing such goons from influential families
 mujhe lagata he ki agar ham jaise kuch visheshadhikaar vaale log bhi aise aparaadhiyon ke saamne nahin khadey honge to bharat main koi khadaa nahin ho paaegaa
 Even more, if i do not stand with my daughter completely in this matter, then i will fail in my duty to be her father
 main do vajahon se ye maamla aapke saath saajha kar rahaa hum

 ' There is also an association of IAS officers
 isane twit kar khanaapurti kar di he

 shaayad vahaan yah faisla ho rahaa hoga ki ham raajnneetik vafadari dikhaaen yaa phir apane peshey ke prati vafadari dikhaaen
 They also know that nothing has to change now
 kyon bhavukta main pratikriya den, isse acha he apni raajnneetik vafadari ke saath rahen

 system main bhi sab unheen ke liye he jo satta ke saath hai

 ab vah itani sad gai he ki diwaar se kaai darak kar gir rahi he
 IAS Virender Kumar has decided to support his daughter
 aaropee bete ke saath iees virendra kumaar se zyada log hai
 Media trials should be avoided
 lekin system kaa media trial to hona hi chahie

 isiilie kisi ko elaan karnaa padataa he ki vah ladega

 is elaan kii apni keemat he

 insaaf or nyaay par bharosa sirf baat nahin he, laagat he

 aap kisi bhi adaalat ke baahar jaakar is bharose ko jeetne aae logon se miliye

 At least 18 states and union territories, including Gujarat, failed to implement the National Food Security Act within the stipulated deadline of September 30, leaving a large section of the poor deprived of the facility to get food grains at very cheap prices
 
 in rajyon ne aakhri vakt main baaji maarijabaki itani hi sankhya main rajyon or kendra shasit pradeshon ne is kanoon ko lagu kar diya he
 States like Telangana, Uttarakhand, Jharkhand, Tripura, Lakshadweep and Pondicherry were able to do this at the last moment
 teen baar badhaai ja chuki thi dedliiskaanoon ko sansad main saal 2013 main paas kiya gayatha or rajya sarkaron ko is yojana ko lagu karne ke liye ek saal kaa samay diya gaya tha
 Thereafter the implementation deadline was extended three times
 aakhri bazaar kii samaysima buudhvaar ko khatm ho gai
 a senior Food Ministry official said, “despite giving more than two years to 50 percent of the total states and union territories, this law has not yet been implemented
 isaki samaysima khatm ho chuki he or ise aage badhaayaa nahin gaya he
 Aiming to benefit two-thirds of the population through the law, the Food Safety Act gives two-thirds of the country's legal right to buy five kg of food grains from ration shops at the rate of one to three rupees per kg per person per month
